                    <h1>
                       Apfel Crumble &#8211; Apple Crumble                    </h1>
                </div>
                <div class="hero-body">
                   <p>Gibt es an einem kühlen Herbsttag etwas Besseres als einen heißen, köstlich duftenden, frisch aus dem Ofen kommenden, Apfel Crumble? Nicht wirklich, oder? Ich liebe ja Crumble in mit jeder Art von Obst, sei es als Marillen Crumble, Zwetschken Crumble oder eben einen Apfel Crumble. Wenn sich Gäste spontan ankündigen, dann ist der Apfel Crumble [&hellip;]</p>

                                            <div id="rezept"></div><div id="recipe"></div><div id="wprm-recipe-container-21376" class="wprm-recipe-container" data-recipe-id="21376" data-servings="2"><div class="wprm-recipe wprm-recipe-template-sweets--lifestyle-2025"><section class="mediterraner-section sweets-lifestyle-recipe">
    <div class="container">
        <div class="row">
            
            <div class="col-xl-8 col-lg-7">
                <div class="mediterraner-content-wrapper">
                    <div class="mediterraner-tag">
                        <p>
                           <span class="wprm-recipe-course wprm-block-text-normal">Dessert</span>

                    <div class="mediterraner-title">
                        <h2 class="wprm-recipe-name wprm-block-text-normal">Apfel Crumble - Apple Crumble</h2>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mediterraner-body">
                        <p>
                          <div class="wprm-recipe-summary wprm-block-text-normal"><span style="display: block;">Apfel Crumble Rezept Ein Apfel Crumble - Apple Crumble - ist einfaches, schnelles und leckeres Dessert. Zum Apfel Crumble passt Vanilleeis und Vanillesauce.</span></div>
<a href="#" role="button" style="color: #333333;" class="wprm-recipe-cook-mode wprm-recipe-link wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe-id="21376" data-modal-uid="2">Kochmodus aktivieren</a>
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

Abrieb"><label for="wprm-checkbox-13" class="wprm-checkbox-label"><span class="sr-only screen-reader-text wprm-screen-reader-text">&#x25a2; </span></label></span><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Zitrone</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded">Bio! Abrieb</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: none;"><span class="wprm-checkbox-container"><input type="checkbox" id="wprm-checkbox-14" class="wprm-checkbox" aria-label="&nbsp;100&#032;g&#032;Mehl"><label for="wprm-checkbox-14" class="wprm-checkbox-label"><span class="sr-only screen-reader-text wprm-screen-reader-text">&#x25a2; </span></label></span><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">100</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">g</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Mehl</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: none;"><span class="wprm-checkbox-container"><input type="checkbox" id="wprm-checkbox-15" class="wprm-checkbox" aria-label="&nbsp;3&#032;Äpfel "><label for="wprm-checkbox-15" class="wprm-checkbox-label"><span class="sr-only screen-reader-text wprm-screen-reader-text">&#x25a2; </span></label></span><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Äpfel </span></li></ul></div></div>
                    </div>
                </div>

              <div class="sweetsandlifestyle-ads-in-recipes">
                <div id="sweetsandlifestyle.com_recipe_1"></div>
              </div>
              
                <div class="mediterraner-recipe-list-2">
                    <div class="list-wrapper">
                            <div id="recipe-21376-instructions" class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-recipe-21376-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe="21376"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-normal wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Zubereitung</h3><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group"><ul class="wprm-recipe-instructions"><li id="wprm-recipe-21376-step-0-0" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Das Backrohr auf 180 Grad Ober- und Unterhitze vorheizen.&nbsp;<br /></span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-21376-step-0-1" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Die Äpfel waschen, schälen, das Kerngehäuse entfernen und die Äpfel in kleine Würfel schneiden. Mit 20g braunem Zucker vermengen.</span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-21376-step-0-2" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Zwei Keramikförmchen (20 cm Ø) fetten und die Apfelmischung darin verteilen.</span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-21376-step-0-3" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Die Butter in kalte Stücke schneiden. Den Kristallzucker mit dem Vanillezucker, Salz, dem Zitronenabrieb, dem Mehl und ggf. mit den Mandelblättchen oder den Walnusshälften mischen. </span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-21376-step-0-4" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Die Butterstücke hinzugeben und zügig zu Streuseln verarbeiten. Den Streuselteig über den Apfelstücken verteilen.</span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-21376-step-0-5" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Den Apfel Crumble 20-25 Minuten backen.</span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-21376-step-0-6" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><span style="display: block;">Den Apfel Crumble aus dem Backrohr nehmen und etwas abkühlen lassen.</span></div></li></ul></div></div>
                    </div>
                  <div id="sweetsandlifestyle.com_mobilebanner_2"> </div>

                    <div class="tip-wrapper">
                        <div class="tip"><div id="recipe-21376-notes" class="wprm-recipe-notes-container wprm-block-text-normal"><div class="wprm-recipe-notes"><span class="suggestion" style="display: block;"><span class="text-gold">Serviervorschlag </span>Den Apfel Crumble mit <a href="https://www.sweetsandlifestyle.com/buchteln-mit-vanillesauce/">selbst gemachter Vanillesauce</a> oder einer Kugel <a href="https://www.sweetsandlifestyle.com/vanilleeis/">Vanilleeis</a> servieren.</span></div></div></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

</section></div></div>
                        <div class='code-block code-block-1' style='margin: 8px 0; clear: both;'>
<div class="symplr-banner symplr-banner-incontent_1">
  <div id="sweetsandlifestyle.com_incontent_1"></div>
</div>
</div>

<p>Gibt es an einem kühlen Herbsttag etwas Besseres als einen heißen, köstlich duftenden, frisch aus dem Ofen kommenden, Apfel Crumble? Nicht wirklich, oder? Ich liebe ja Crumble in mit jeder Art von Obst, sei es als <a href="https://www.sweetsandlifestyle.com/marillen-crumble/">Marillen Crumble</a>, <a href="https://www.sweetsandlifestyle.com/zwetschken-crumble/">Zwetschken Crumble</a> oder eben einen Apfel Crumble. </p>



<p>Wenn sich Gäste spontan ankündigen, dann ist der Apfel Crumble eines einfaches, schnelles Dessert, welches binnen 30 Minuten fertig ist. Und während der Crumble im Backrohr ist, mache ich gerne noch eine Vanillesauce. Denn am liebsten serviere ich den Apfel Crumble mit Vanillesauce. Manchmal gibt es auch eine Kugel Vanilleeis anstatt der Sauce dazu.</p>



<div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter"><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20683%201024'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Leckerer Apfel Crumble mit Vanillesauce serviert von Sweets &amp; <script data-minify="1" type="text/javascript" src="https://www.sweetsandlifestyle.com/wp-content/cache/min/1/wp-content/themes/sweets-and-lifestyle/js/scripts.js?ver=1771850194" id="sweets-lifestyle-js" data-rocket-defer defer></script>
<script type="text/javascript" id="wprm-cookmode-de-fix-js-after">
/* <![CDATA[ */
(function () {
  function setTextIfEquals(el, from, to) {
    if (!el) return;
    const current = (el.textContent || '').trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
    if (current === from) el.textContent = to;
  }

  function setAttrIfEquals(el, attr, from, to) {
    if (!el) return;
    const current = (el.getAttribute(attr) || '').trim();
    if (current === from) el.setAttribute(attr, to);
  }

  function translateCookMode(root) {
    root = root || document;

    root.querySelectorAll('.wprm-cook-mode-start-button').forEach(btn => {
      const t = (btn.textContent || '').trim();
      if (t === 'Start Cooking') btn.textContent = 'Kochen starten';
    });

    root.querySelectorAll('.wprm-cook-mode-control-label').forEach(label => {
      setTextIfEquals(label, 'Servings', 'Portionen');
    });

    root.querySelectorAll('.wprm-cook-mode-nav-prev').forEach(btn => {
      const raw = (btn.textContent || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
      if (raw.endsWith('Previous')) btn.textContent = raw.replace(/Previous$/, 'Zurück');
      setAttrIfEquals(btn, 'aria-label', 'Previous step', 'Zurück');
    });

    root.querySelectorAll('.wprm-cook-mode-nav-next').forEach(btn => {
      const raw = (btn.textContent || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
      if (raw.startsWith('Next')) btn.textContent = raw.replace(/^Next/, 'Weiter');
      else if (raw.endsWith('Next')) btn.textContent = raw.replace(/Next$/, 'Weiter');
      setAttrIfEquals(btn, 'aria-label', 'Next step', 'Weiter');
    });

    root.querySelectorAll('.wprm-popup-modal__close').forEach(btn => {
      setAttrIfEquals(btn, 'aria-label', 'Close', 'Beenden');
    });

    root.querySelectorAll('.wprm-cook-mode-nav-close').forEach(btn => {
      setTextIfEquals(btn, 'Close', 'Beenden');
      setAttrIfEquals(btn, 'aria-label', 'Close', 'Beenden');
    });

    root.querySelectorAll('.wprm-cook-mode-progress-text').forEach(el => {
      const cur = el.querySelector('.wprm-cook-mode-progress-step-current');
      const tot = el.querySelector('.wprm-cook-mode-progress-step-total');
      if (!cur || !tot) return;
      el.textContent = '';
      el.append('Schritt ', cur, ' von ', tot);
    });
  }

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => translateCookMode(document));
  } else {
    translateCookMode(document);
  }

  const obs = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
    for (const m of mutations) {
      if (m.addedNodes && m.addedNodes.length) {
        m.addedNodes.forEach(node => {
          if (node.nodeType === 1) translateCookMode(node);
        });
      }
    }
  });

  obs.observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();
//# sourceURL=wprm-cookmode-de-fix-js-after
/* ]]> */
</script>
